Index 3 and 632

Advance width of 'thinspace' (uni2009) should be smaller than the advance width of 'space' (uni0020).

Advance width 'thinspace' 153 is smaller than 'space' 200, but should be 60% of space '120.0'. Please verify if this is intend to be like it is.

Info

Baloo Da 2 Regular (BalooDa2-Regular.ttf)

STAT

static font

Variable font must have a STAT table.

No check of STAT table for static fonts included, yet. Static fonts do not need to have a STAT table. It is only recommended by Microsoft, not required.
More infos here:
https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/typography/opentype/spec/stat

Baloo Da 2 Medium Regular (BalooDa2-Medium.ttf)

name

Mac NID 16/17

Mac NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Baloo Da 2' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Baloo Da 2' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Medium'.

Pass

Baloo Da 2 SemiBold Regular (BalooDa2-SemiBold.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'BalooDa2-SemiBold', Everything looks good.

Baloo Da 2 SemiBold Regular (BalooDa2-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'BalooDa2-SemiBold', Everything looks good.

Pass

'space' in NID 6 cause issues in fontbook for Mac.

NID 6 is 'BalooDa2-SemiBold', Everything looks good.

Pass

, most common Monotype license test is:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

Baloo Da 2 SemiBold Regular (BalooDa2-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Baloo Da 2' + 'Space' + NID 17 'SemiBold' = NID 1 'Baloo Da 2 SemiBold'.

Pass

Mac NID 16/17

Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Baloo Da 2' + 'Space' + NID 17 'ExtraBold' = NID 1 'Baloo Da 2' + 'Space' + NID 2 'ExtraBold'.

This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.
